<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">Item 8.01 Other Events</font></font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt">
<br></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">NIKE Brand Operating Segments</font></font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">As previously announced, in the third quarter of fiscal 2009 NIKE, Inc. (the &#8220;Company&#8221;) initiated a reorganization of the NIKE brand into a new model consisting of six geographies.&#160; Beginning in the first quarter of fiscal 2010, the Company&#8217;s new reportable operating segments for the NIKE brand are: North America, Western
Europe, Central/Eastern Europe, Greater China, Japan, and Emerging Markets.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt">
<br></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">The following list contains major countries in each geography.&#160;&#160;Some countries have been excluded due to their relatively small revenue contribution:</font></div>

<td width="25%"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">&#160;<font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">&#9642;&#160; Hungary</font></font></td>
<td width="25%"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">&#160;<font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">&#9642;&#160; Turkey</font></font></td>

<td width="25%"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">&#160;</font></td>
<td width="25%"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">&#160;</font></td>
<td width="25%"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">&#160;</font></td>
<td width="25%"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">&#160;</font></td></tr></table></div>
<div>&#160;</div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left">&#160;</div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">Change of Primary Financial Measure</font></font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Effective June 1, 2009, the primary financial measure used by the Company to evaluate performance of individual operating segments is Earnings Before Interest and Taxes (&#8220;EBIT&#8221;) which represents net income before interest income, net and income taxes.&#160; Previously, the Company evaluated performance of individual operating segments
based on income before income taxes (previously referred to as &#8220;Pre-tax Income&#8221;).&#160; Financial information has been restated to conform to the new primary financial measure used by the Company.&#160;</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt">
<br></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">Unaudited, Reclassified Operating Segment Data</font></font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">The Company is filing this Current Report on Form 8-K to reclassify historical segment information in accordance with the Company&#8217;s current segment structure and to reflect the change in the primary financial measure used by the Company to evaluate performance of individual operating segments as discussed above.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt">
<br></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Exhibits 99.1 and 99.2 to this Current Report on Form 8-K provide a summary of the effects of the above reclassification of historical segment information on the Company&#8217;s historical segment results.</font></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt">
<br></div>
<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">The changes in the segment structure and primary financial measure discussed above, in this Current Report on Form 8-K, affect only the manner in which the results for the operating segments were previously reported. These reclassifications have no impact on the Company&#8217;s previously reported consolidated statements of income, balance
sheets, statements of cash flows and statements of shareholders&#8217; equity. The information in this Current Report on Form 8-K, including Exhibit 99.1 and 99.2, should be read in conjunction with the Company&#8217;s Annual Report on Form 10-K for the fiscal year ended May 31, 2009, which was filed with the Security and Exchange Commission on July 27, 2009.</font></div>

or shareholders' equity.</div>
<div style="LINE-HEIGHT: 0.5">&#160;</div>
<div><font style="FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top">4 </font>Global Brand Divisions primarily represent NIKE Brand licensing businesses that are not part of a geographic operating segment and general and administrative expenses that are centrally managed for the NIKE Brand.</div>
<div style="LINE-HEIGHT: 0.5">&#160;</div>
<div><font style="FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top">5</font> Other Businesses represents activities of Cole Haan, Converse, Exeter Brands Group (whose primary business was the Starter brand business which was sold December 17, 2007), Hurley, NIKE Bauer Hockey (through April 16, 2008), NIKE Golf, and Umbro (beginning March 3, 2008).</div>
<div>&#160;</div>
<div><font style="FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top">6</font> Corporate Expense primarily consists of unallocated general and administrative expenses, which includes expenses associated with centrally managed departments, depreciation and amortization related to the Company's corporate headquarters, unallocated insurance and benefit programs, foreign currency gains and losses, including hedge gains and losses, corporate eliminations and other items.<br></div></body>
